# 1857 — Divided States of America
country_event = {
	id = usa_intro.1
	title = usa_intro.1.t
	desc = usa_intro.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_election_generic

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_intro.1"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
						name = usa_intro.1.a
		# log = "option:						name = usa_intro.1.a"
						trigger = { is_ai = no }
						country_event = usa_intro.2
	}
	option = {
						name = usa_intro.1.b
		# log = "option:						name = usa_intro.1.b"
						trigger = { is_ai = no }
						country_event = usa_intro.3
	}
	option = {
						 name = usa_intro.1.c
		# log = "option:						 name = usa_intro.1.c"
						 trigger = { is_ai = no }
						 country_event = usa_intro.4
	}
	option = {
		name = usa_intro.1.e
		# log = "option:		name = usa_intro.1.e"
		add_political_power = -5
		hidden_effect = {
			360 = { OWNER = { country_event = { id = usa_flavor.2 days = 300 random_days = 100 } } }
		}
	}
}

	id = usa_intro.2 # Seminole War

#####################################
# 1860 New England Shoemaker Strike #
#####################################
country_event = { #New England Shoemakers Cut Wages
	id = usa_worker_events.1
	title = usa_worker_events.1.t
	desc = usa_worker_events.1.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.1.a"
	}
}
state_event = { #1860
	id = usa_worker_events.2
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_worker_events.2"
		OWNER = { country_event = { id = usa_worker_events.3 } }
	}
}
country_event = { #Mechanics Association Formed
	id = usa_worker_events.3
	title = usa_worker_events.3.t
	desc = usa_worker_events.3.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_worker_events.3"
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_worker_events.4 days = 7 }
			news_event = { id = usa_worker_events.5 days = 170 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.3.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.3.a"
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_egalitarianism popularity = 0.01 }
		#worker organization increase
	}
	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.3.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.3.b"
		trigger = { has_political_power > 0 }
		add_political_power = -50
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_egalitarianism popularity = 0.03 }
		#worker organization increase
	}
}
news_event = { #Shoemaker Strike Begins
	id = usa_worker_events.4
	title = usa_worker_events.4.t
	desc = usa_worker_events.4.d
	show_major = {
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
			TAG = USA
			is_subject_of = USA
		}
		else = {
			NA_B_is_american_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.4.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.4.a"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 357
				owns_state = 960
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.4.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.4.b"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 357
				owns_state = 960
			}
		}
	}
}
news_event = { #Shoemaker Strike Ends
	id = usa_worker_events.5
	title = usa_worker_events.5.t
	desc = usa_worker_events.5.d
	show_major = {
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
			TAG = USA
			is_subject_of = USA
		}
		else = {
			NA_B_is_american_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_worker_events.5.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_worker_events.5.a"
	}
}


####################### Western Expansion Events ##########################

###############################
# 1858 — Pikes Peak Gold Rush #
###############################
state_event = {
	id = usa_western_expansion.1
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_western_expansion.1"
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { afr_is_tribal_allowed = yes } }
			OWNER = { country_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.3 days = 7 } }
			if = {
				limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
				OWNER = { news_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.2 } }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = { news_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.2 } }
		}
	}
}
news_event = { #Non-Native
	id = usa_western_expansion.2
	title = usa_western_expansion.2.t
	desc = usa_western_expansion.2.d
	show_major = {
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
			TAG = USA
			is_subject_of = USA
		}
		else = {
			NA_B_is_american_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_western_expansion.2.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_western_expansion.2.a"
		if = {
			limit = { TAG = USA }
			complete_national_focus = USA_FN_pike_peak_gold_rush
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Native
	id = usa_western_expansion.4
	title = usa_western_expansion.4.t

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_western_expansion.4.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_western_expansion.4.a"
	}
}

#####################################
### The Iron Horse Reaches Kansas ###
#####################################
state_event = {
	id = usa_western_expansion.6
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_western_expansion.6"
		OWNER = {
			news_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.7 }
			every_country = {
				limit = { afr_is_tribal_allowed = yes }
				country_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.8 days = 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}
news_event = { #US - The Iron Horse Reaches Kansas
	id = usa_western_expansion.7
	title = usa_western_expansion.7.t
	desc = usa_western_expansion.7.d
	show_major = {
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
			TAG = USA
			is_subject_of = USA
		}
		else = {
			NA_B_is_american_allowed = yes
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_western_expansion.7.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_western_expansion.7.a"
		if = {
			limit = { TAG = USA }
			complete_national_focus = USA_FN_growing_rail_industry
		}
	}
}

state_event = {
	id = usa_western_expansion.13
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_western_expansion.13"
		OWNER = {
			news_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.14 }
			every_country = {
				limit = { afr_is_tribal_allowed = yes }
				country_event = { id = usa_western_expansion.15 days = 7 }
			}
		}
	}
}
news_event = { #US - Agricultural Breakthrough
	id = usa_western_expansion.14
	title = usa_western_expansion.14.t
	desc = usa_western_expansion.14.d
	show_major = {
		if = {
			limit = { USA = { exists = yes } }
			TAG = USA
			is_subject_of = USA
			if = {
				limit = { CSA = { exists = yes } }
				TAG = CSA
			}
		}
		else = {
			NA_B_is_american_allowed = yes
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_western_expansion.14.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_western_expansion.14.a"
		if = {
			limit = { TAG = USA }
			complete_national_focus = USA_FN_americas_breadbasket
		}
	}
}

####################### Panic of 1857 ##########################

# Panic of 1857 2
country_event = {
	id = usa_panic.1
	title = usa_panic.1.t
	desc = usa_panic.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally2

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_panic.1"
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_panic.1.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_panic.1.a"
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				# industrial_complex > 0
				is_core_of = USA
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						size@token:railway > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:port > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:steel_foundry > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:mechanical_works > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:chemical_plant > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:tooling_workshop > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:consumer_goods_factory > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:textile_mill > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:entertainment_hub > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:crop_farm > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:rice_paddy > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:livestock_ranch > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:cotton_plantation > 0
					}
						check_variable = {
						size@token:luxuries_plantation > 0
					}
				}

			}
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:railway < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:railway < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:railway }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:port < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:port < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:port }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:steel_foundry < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:steel_foundry < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:steel_foundry }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:mechanical_works < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:mechanical_works < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:mechanical_works }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:chemical_plant < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:chemical_plant < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:chemical_plant }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:tooling_workshop < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:tooling_workshop < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:tooling_workshop }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:consumer_goods_factory < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						check_variable = { size@token:consumer_goods_factory < 1 }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { industry_token = token:consumer_goods_factory }
					set_temp_variable = { x_temp = 1 }
					remove_x_industries = yes
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						check_variable = { size@token:textile_mill < 2 }
					}
					modifier = {

country_event = {#sets AI behavior
	id = USA_utah_war.50
	title = USA_utah_war.50.t
	desc = USA_utah_war.50.d
	#hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA_utah_war.50.a
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.50.a"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_mormon_NME
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_peaceful
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					85 = {
						set_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_peaceful
					}
					15 = {
						set_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_aggressive
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_NME

			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
			set_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
			set_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_peaceful
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#reduce by 2
		name = USA_utah_war.26.b
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.26.b"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_NME
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = USA_utah_war.23
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
		set_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_peaceful
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = {
					USA_mormon_unrest > 10
				}
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#increase by 1
		name = USA_utah_war.26.c
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.26.c"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = USA_utah_war.20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
			}
			clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
			set_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
			set_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = AI_USA_mormonWar_aggressive
				factor = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {#increase by 2
		name = USA_utah_war.26.e
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.26.e"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
				has_country_flag = USA_mormon_MME
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = USA_utah_war.21
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_mormon_SME
		set_country_flag = USA_mormon_LME
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10

				every_owned_state = {

				}
			}
		}
		USA = {
			transfer_state = 382
			transfer_state = 1092
			transfer_state = 380
			transfer_state = 379
			transfer_state = 258
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				1291 = {
					is_owned_by = USA
				}
			}
			SHO = {
				transfer_state = 1291
			}
		}
		country_event = usa.65
	}

country_event = {#ongoing event which adds mormon unrest forcing the player to do something, with failsafes
	id = USA_utah_war.98
	title = USA_utah_war.98.t
	desc = {
		text = USA_utah_war.98.d1
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = USA_utah_war.98.d2
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing }
			}
		}
	}		#USA_utah_war.98.d is taken by an option

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no

	option = {
		name = USA_utah_war.98.a
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.98.a"
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 5
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 0
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_mormon_unrest
			value = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA_utah_war.98 days = 35 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						UTA = {
							is_puppet_of = USA
						}
						USA = {
							check_variable = {
								var = USA_mormon_unrest
								value = 5
								compare = greater_than_or_equals
							}
						}
					}
				}
				USA = {
					country_event = { id = USA_utah_war.97 days = 1 }

				}
			}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_utah_war.98.b
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.98.b"
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 10
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 5
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_mormon_unrest
			value = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			country_event = { id = USA_utah_war.98 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_utah_war.98.c
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.98.c"
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
				}
				check_variable = { USA_mormon_unrest < 18 }
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 10
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_mormon_unrest
			value = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA_utah_war.98 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_utah_war.98.d
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.98.d"
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
				}
				check_variable = { USA_mormon_unrest < 0 }
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = USA_mormon_unrest
			value = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA_utah_war.98 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = {# failsafe layer 1
		name = USA_utah_war.98.e
		# log = "option:		name = USA_utah_war.98.e"
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 75
	}
}

			}
		}

			add_country_leader_role = {

		}

	}

	id = usaPolitics.5
		title = usaPolitics.5.t
		desc = usaPolitics.5.desc
		picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	immediate = {

				id = usaPolitics.3
				days = 123
			}

			}

	}

		name = usaPolitics.5.a

			add_country_leader_role = {

country_event = { # 1872 Democratic National Convention
	id = usaPolitics.7
		title = usaPolitics.7.t
		desc = usaPolitics.7.desc
		picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usaPolitics.7"
	}
		is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usaPolitics.7"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = usaPolitics.8
				days = 1437
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Current President
		name = usaPolitics.7.a
		# log = "option:		name = usaPolitics.7.a"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = traditional_conservatism
				has_government = radical_democracy
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = { # Horace Greeley
		name = usaPolitics.7.b
		# log = "option:		name = usaPolitics.7.b"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = traditional_conservatism
					has_government = radical_democracy
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = USA_liberal_republicans_formed
		}
		USA_character_horace_greeley = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					ideology = conserv_liberal
					expire = "1872.11.29"
					traits = { influencial_writer }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				centrism < 0.25
			}
			set_temp_variable = { usapolitics_centrism_diff = 0.25 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { usapolitics_centrism_diff = party_popularity@centrism }
			add_to_temp_variable = { usapolitics_centrism_diff = 0.02 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = centrism
				popularity = var:usapolitics_centrism_diff
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				traditional_conservatism > 0.25
			}
			set_temp_variable = { usapolitics_traditional_conservatism_diff = party_popularity@traditional_conservatism }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { usapolitics_traditional_conservatism_diff = 0.20 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { usapolitics_traditional_conservatism_diff = -1 }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = traditional_conservatism
				popularity = var:usapolitics_traditional_conservatism_diff
			}
		}
		set_variable = { usa_centrism_candidate = token:USA_character_horace_greeley }
	}
}

# Call Up to Arms
country_event = {
	id = usa.14
	title = usa.14.t
	desc = usa.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_military_parade

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.14"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.14.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.14.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_Radical_Coup
			}
			load_oob = USA_CIVIL_WAR_RADICAL
			hidden_effect = {
				set_division_template_lock = {
					division_template = "Union Regimental"
					is_locked = yes
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			load_oob = USA_CIVIL_WAR
			hidden_effect = {
				set_division_template_lock = {
					division_template = "Union Regimental"
					is_locked = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Peace!
country_event = {
	id = usa.18
	title = usa.18.t
	desc = usa.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.18"
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.18.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.18.a"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		#remove_ideas = american_slavery_3
		add_political_power = 250
		add_timed_idea = { idea = usa_thirty_year_plan_1 days = 3650 }
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = usa_news.8 }
			USA = {
				country_event = { days = 3561 id = usa.21 }
			}
			set_global_flag = ACW_Civil_War_Avoided
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.2
	title = usa_event_check.2.t
	desc = usa_event_check.2.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.2"
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_war_with = CSA
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = autocracy
							has_government = vanguard_communism
							has_government = collectivist_socialism
							has_government = anarchism
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.36
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = CSA
						has_government = autocracy
						has_government = vanguard_communism
						has_government = collectivist_socialism
						has_government = anarchism
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.38
		}
		else = { }
	}
}

#Alaska Russia
country_event = {
	id = usa.41
	title = usa.41.t
	desc = usa.41.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.41"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.41.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.41.a"
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.42 hours = 1 } }
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_alaska_purchase_rus days = 365 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = sold_alaska_target
			set_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus
		}
		set_global_flag = USAAlaska_Purchased
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.41.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.41.b"
		add_political_power = -25
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.42 hours = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
	}

		}
	}

			factor = 70

				factor = 0

			}
		}

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.8"

				}
			}
			country_event = usa.86
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.8
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = usa_event_check.11.t
	desc = usa_event_check.11.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.11"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.11"
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					has_country_flag = USA_first_kkk
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.89
		}
	}
}
#KKK intimidates voters
country_event = {
	id = usa.89
	title = usa.89.t
	desc = usa.89.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.89"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.89"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.12
				days = 20
				random_days = 40
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.89.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.89.a"
		add_to_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 1
		}
		add_manpower = -2500
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_add_1
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_plus_1 = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = centrism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_government = social_egalitarianism
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.89.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.89.b"
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 4
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_remove_4
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_minus_4 = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = centrism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_government = traditional_conservatism
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.12
	title = usa_event_check.12.t
	desc = usa_event_check.12.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.12"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.12"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_first_kkk
				any_owned_state = {
					industrial_complex > 0
					OR = {
						state = 362
						state = 363
						state = 364
						state = 365
						state = 366
						state = 367
						state = 368
						state = 370
						state = 371
						state = 372
						state = 375
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = usa.90
				days = 1
				random_days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}
#KKK disrupts southern factory
country_event = {
	id = usa.90
	title = usa.90.t
	desc = usa.90.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.90"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.90.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.90.a"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_to_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_add_1
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_plus_1 = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = centrism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				AND = {
					has_government = social_egalitarianism
					is_historical_focus_on = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				AND = {
					check_variable = { reconstruction_points < 70 }
					is_historical_focus_on = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.90.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.90.b"
		add_political_power = -25
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
				OR = {
					state = 362
					state = 363
					state = 364
					state = 365
					state = 366
					state = 367
					state = 368
					state = 370
					state = 371
					state = 372
					state = 375
				}
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 0.5
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 1
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = centrism
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_remove_1
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_minus_1 = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.90.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.90.c"
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
				OR = {
					state = 362
					state = 363
					state = 364
					state = 365
					state = 366
					state = 367
					state = 368
					state = 370
					state = 371
					state = 372
					state = 375
				}
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 2
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				has_government = centrism
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_government = traditional_conservatism
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_remove_2
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_minus_2 = yes
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.13
	title = usa_event_check.13
	desc = usa_event_check.13
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.13"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.13"
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { reconstruction_points > 24 }
				has_country_flag = USA_first_kkk
			}
			country_event = usa.91
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_first_kkk
			}
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.13
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

#Reconstruction is Over
country_event = {
	id = usa.95
	title = usa.95.t
	desc = usa.95.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.95"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.95"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_standard_oil_influence
				value = 47
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_standard_oil_popularity
				value = 59
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
				value = 50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_steel_influence
				value = 43
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_steel_popularity
				value = 64
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = USA_steel_opinion
				value = 50
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.95.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.95.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points > 99
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = limited_equality
			add_idea = full_equality
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_enforcement_act
		set_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.95.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.95.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points < 100
			}
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points > 79
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_enforcement_act
		set_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
		load_focus_tree = usa_gilded_age
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.95.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.95.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points < 80
			}
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points > 19
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = limited_equality
			add_idea = segregation
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_enforcement_act
		set_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
		load_focus_tree = usa_gilded_age
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.95.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.95.a"
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				reconstruction_points < 20
			}
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = limited_equality
			add_idea = racial_laws
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_enforcement_act
		set_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
		load_focus_tree = usa_gilded_age
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usa.96
	title = usa.96.t
	desc = usa.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.96"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.96.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.96.a"
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = lp_land_purchase
			add_idea = lp_land_estates
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.96.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.96.b"
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

#Recognize Emperor Norton?
country_event = {
	id = usa.98
	title = usa.98.t
	desc = usa.98.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.98"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.98.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.98.a"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = usa_recognize_norton
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = usa_recognize_norton
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.98.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.98.b"
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = usa_refuse_norton
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = USA
			modifier = usa_refuse_norton
		}
	}
}

#West Virginia Ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = usa.105
	title = usa.105.t
	desc = usa.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.105"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.105.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.105.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio > 1.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio > 5 }
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = USA_CSA_westvirginia
			country_event = { id = usa.108 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.105.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.105.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio < 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio < 0.5 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				strength_ratio = { tag = USA ratio < 0.2 }
			}
		}
		USA = {
			country_event = { id = usa.107 }
		}
	}
}

#Ultimatum Accepted
country_event = {
	id = usa.108
	title = usa.108.t
	desc = usa.108.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.108"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.108.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.108.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_CSA_westvirginia
			}
			transfer_state = 746
			add_state_core = 746
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USA_CSA_arizona
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CSA = { owns_state = 377 }
				}
				transfer_state = 377
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					CSA = { owns_state = 1286 }
				}
				transfer_state = 1286
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = usa_event_check.15.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.15"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.15"
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					OR = {
						owns_state = 1306
						owns_state = 375
						owns_state = 1304
						owns_state = 1281
						owns_state = 1280
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.109
		}
		else = { }
	}
}

		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.115"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.115.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.115.a"
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = usa.116 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.115.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.115.b"
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.112 days = 5 }
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = usa.116 days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.115.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.115.c"

	}

#MHC Election
country_event = {
	id = usa.122
	title = usa.122.t
	desc = usa.122.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.122"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.122"
		set_variable = {
			var = MHC_anarchism_points
			value = party_popularity@anarchism
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = MHC_social_points
			value = party_popularity@social_egalitarianism
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = MHC_collective_points
			value = party_popularity@collectivist_socialism
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = MHC_communist_points
			value = party_popularity@vanguard_communism
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.122.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.122.a"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points > MHC_social_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points = MHC_social_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points > MHC_collective_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points = MHC_collective_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points > MHC_communist_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_anarchism_points = MHC_communist_points }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = anarchism
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_mhc_warren_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.122.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.122.b"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points > MHC_anarchism_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points = MHC_anarchism_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points > MHC_collective_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points = MHC_collective_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points > MHC_communist_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_social_points = MHC_communist_points }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_egalitarianism
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_mhc_uriah_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.122.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.122.c"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points > MHC_anarchism_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points = MHC_anarchism_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points > MHC_social_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points = MHC_social_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points > MHC_communist_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_collective_points = MHC_communist_points }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = collectivist_socialism
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_mhc_sorge_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.122.e
		# log = "option:		name = usa.122.e"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points > MHC_social_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points = MHC_social_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points > MHC_collective_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points = MHC_collective_points }
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points > MHC_anarchism_points }
				check_variable = { MHC_communist_points = MHC_anarchism_points }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = vanguard_communism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_country_flag = USA_mhc_dietzgen_flag
	}
}

#USA Purchase of Iceland/Greenland 1867
country_event = {
	id = usa.146
	title = usa.146.t
	desc = usa.146.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.146"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.146.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.146.a"
		ai_chance = {
				factor = 70
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_country = {
					owns_state = 101
					NOT = { owns_state = 100}
				}
			}
			101 = {
				owner = { country_event = { id = usa.149 hours = 1 } }
			}
			100 = {
				owner = { country_event = { id = usa.150 hours = 1 } }
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_purchasing_greenland
			set_country_flag = USA_purchasing_iceland
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 101
					owns_state = 100
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.147 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.146.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.146.b"
		ai_chance = {
				factor = 30
			}
	}
}
#USA Purchase FROM Response (BOTH)
country_event = {
	id = usa.147
	title = usa.147.t
	desc = usa.147.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.147"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.147.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.147.a"
		ai_chance = {
				factor = 10
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_accept
			country_event = { id = usa.148 hours = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.147.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.147.b"
		ai_chance = {
				factor = 40
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
			country_event = { id = usa.148 hours = 1 }
		}
	}

#USA Gets Response
country_event = {
	id = usa.148
	title = usa.148.t
	desc = usa.148.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.148"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.148.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.148.a"
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
					has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland
				}
				has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_accept
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = USA_DEN_sold_icegreen
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		USA = {
			transfer_state = 101
			transfer_state = 100
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_accept
		news_event = { id = usa_news.25 }
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.148.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.148.b"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		USA = {
			transfer_state = 101
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
		clr_country_flag = USA_purchasing_greenland
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = USA_purchasing_greenland
							has_country_flag = USA_purchasing_iceland
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = USA_DEN_sold_green
				news_event = { id = usa_news.25 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.148.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.148.c"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_accept }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland }
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.148.e
		# log = "option:		name = usa.148.e"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		USA = {
			transfer_state = 100
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland
		clr_country_flag = USA_purchasing_iceland
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = USA_purchasing_greenland
							has_country_flag = USA_purchasing_iceland
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = USA_DEN_sold_ice
				news_event = { id = usa_news.25 }
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = usa.149.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.149.a"
		ai_chance = {
				factor = 50
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_greenland
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = USA_purchasing_iceland
						}
						has_country_flag = USA_DEN_icebox_iceland
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = usa.148 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

				factor = 50
				modifier = {

### Gilded Age Events ###
country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.19
	title = usa_event_check.19.t
	desc = usa_event_check.19.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.19"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.19"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_opinion
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1876.1.1
						date < 1877.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1880.1.1
						date < 1881.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1884.1.1
						date < 1885.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1888.1.1
						date < 1889.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1892.1.1
						date < 1893.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1896.1.1
						date < 1897.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1900.1.1
						date < 1900.1.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.151
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.19
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}
#Captians of Industry events
country_event = {
	id = usa.151
	title = usa.151.t
	desc = usa.151.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.151"
	}

	trigger = {########### this should be triggered differently
		has_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
		tag = USA
		OR = {
			check_variable = {
				var = USA_steel_opinion
				value = 40
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
				value = 40
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1876.1.1
				date < 1877.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1880.1.1
				date < 1881.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1884.1.1
				date < 1885.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1888.1.1
				date < 1889.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1892.1.1
				date < 1893.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1896.1.1
				date < 1897.1.1
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1900.1.1
				date < 1900.1.1
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_steel_opinion
					value = 30
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
					value = 30
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_steel_opinion
					value = 30
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
					value = 30
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.151.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.151.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_opinion
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_influence
						value = 20
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = traditional_conservatism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = traditional_conservatism
					popularity = -0.01
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = centrism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = centrism
					popularity = -0.01
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_egalitarianism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_egalitarianism
					popularity = -0.01
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = radical_democracy
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_democracy
					popularity = -0.01
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_opinion
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_influence
						value = 40
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_influence
						value = 20
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {

country_event = { #Recurring Event Check for Person dies from conditions
	id = usa_event_check.16
	title = usa_event_check.16.t
	desc = usa_event_check.16.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.16"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.16"
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = eight_hour_work_day
					}
					has_idea = cl_illegal
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.152
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.16
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = cl_illegal
					}
					has_idea = eight_hour_work_day
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.153
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.16
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = cl_illegal
						has_idea = eight_hour_work_day
					}
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = usa.152
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = usa.153
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.16
				days = 30
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				USA = {
					has_idea = cl_illegal
					has_idea = eight_hour_work_day
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.16
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}
#Person dies from conditions
country_event = {
	id = usa.152
	title = usa.152.t
	desc = usa.152.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.152"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.152"
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = USA
				}
				save_event_target_as = USA_gilded_facdeath_state
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa.152.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.152.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_opinion_steel_2
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_opinion_oil_2
		add_political_power = 25
		clear_global_event_target = USA_gilded_facdeath_state
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.152.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.152.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_opinion_steel_2
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_opinion_oil_2
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_popularity
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_popularity
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_popularity_steel_2
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_popularity
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_popularity_oil_2
		clear_global_event_target = USA_gilded_facdeath_state
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.17
	title = usa_event_check.17.t
	desc =	usa_event_check.17.desc
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.17"
	}
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.17"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_opinion
						value = 60
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
						value = 60
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1876.1.1
						date < 1877.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1880.1.1
						date < 1881.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1884.1.1
						date < 1885.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1888.1.1
						date < 1889.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1892.1.1
						date < 1893.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1896.1.1
						date < 1897.1.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1900.1.1
						date < 1900.1.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = usa.154
				days = 30
				random_days = 90
			}
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.17
				days = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

					ideology = traditional_conservatism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = centrism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = centrism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_egalitarianism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_egalitarianism
					popularity = 0.04
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = radical_democracy
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_democracy
					popularity = 0.04
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
						value = 60
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_influence
						value = 100
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_influence
						value = 80
						compare = greater_than
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = traditional_conservatism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = traditional_conservatism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = centrism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = centrism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_egalitarianism
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_egalitarianism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = radical_democracy
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = radical_democracy
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = usa_event_check.18
	title = usa_event_check.18.t
	desc = usa_event_check.18.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = placeholder

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.18"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_event_check.18"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_steel_popularity
						value = 40
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_standard_oil_popularity
						value = 40
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = usa.156
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = USA_gilded_age_ft } }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_event_check.18
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

	}

				factor = 100

			}

				}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SPR
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Annexation of Santo Domingo
country_event = {
	id = usa.167
	title = usa.167.t
	desc = usa.167.d
	picture = GFX_santo_domingo

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.167"
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {########### this should be triggered differently
		tag = USA
		date > 1869.01.01
		date < 1872.12.31
		DOM={
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
		}
	}

	option = { #Annex
		name = usa.167.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.167.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				has_government = social_egalitarianism
				factor = 80
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		annex_country = {
			target = DOM
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 4
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_add_4
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_plus_4 = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Sphere of Inf
		name = usa.167.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.167.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		puppet = DOM
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = 2
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_add_2
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				has_autonomy_state = autonomy_unintegrated_seceded_state
			}
			USAROD_reconstruction_progress_plus_2 = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Refuse (Historical)
		name = usa.167.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.167.c"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = reconstruction_points
			value = -2
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_reconstruction_remove_2
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {

#Compromise of 1877
country_event = {
	id = usa.185
	title = usa.185.t
	desc = usa.185.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally2

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.185"
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = { ######win_end_reconstruction should trigger this
		# has_completed_focus = USA_win_end_reconstruction
		NOT = {
			has_idea = full_equality
		}
	}

	option = { #Satisfy Democratic demands fully
		name = usa.185.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.185.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -200
		add_stability = 0.04
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = -1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.4
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_democrats_assume_south_fully }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_radical_republicans_collapse}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { days = 20 id = usa.186 } }
	}

	option = { #Satisfy some demands
		name = usa.185.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.185.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_democrats_assume_south_partially }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_radical_republicans_collapse }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { days = 20 id = usa.186 } }
	}

	option = { # Never compromise with Democrats!
		name = usa.185.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.185.c"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = traditional_conservatism
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_republicans_control_south }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_prolonged_radical_republican_era }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { days = 10 id = usa.187 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Creation of the National Union Party
	id = usa.190
	title = usa.190.t
	desc = usa.190.d
	picture = GFX_Lincoln_Johnson

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.190"
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {########## This should be triggered differently
		TAG = USA
		date > 1864.1.1
		date < 1864.4.1
		has_war_with = CSA
		has_country_flag = USA_LincolnElected
	}

	option = { #Form the Union Ticket
		name = usa.190.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.190.a"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = centrism
			long_name = USA_national_union_party_long
			name = USA_national_union_party
		}

		set_party_name = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			long_name = USA_national_union_party_long
			name = USA_national_union_party
		}

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.07
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_democracy
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_war_support = 0.05
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = USA_national_union_party_created }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_egalitarianism
				long_name =	USA_radical_republican_party_long
				name =	USA_radical_republican_party
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Decline the Union Ticket
		name = usa.190.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.190.b"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_democracy
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		add_war_support = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_democracy
				long_name = USA_democratic_party_radical_long
				name = USA_democratic_party_radical
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = traditional_conservatism
				long_name = USA_democratic_party_moderate_long
				name = USA_democratic_party_moderate
			}
		}
	}
}

#Alaska Russia Mormons
country_event = {
	id = usa.212
	title = usa.212.t
	desc = usa.212.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.212"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.212.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.212.a"
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.213 hours = 1 } }
		ROOT = { add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_alaska_purchase_rus_2 days = 365 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = sold_alaska_target
			set_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus
		}
		set_global_flag = USAAlaska_Purchased
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.212.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.212.b"
		add_political_power = -25
		USA = { country_event = { id = usa.213 hours = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
#Alaska Result
country_event = {
	id = usa.213
	title = usa.213.t
	desc = {
		text = usa.213.d1
		trigger = { has_global_flag = USAAlaska_Purchased }
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa.213.d2
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = USAAlaska_Purchased } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.213"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.213.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.213.a"
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = USAAlaska_Purchased
		}
		news_event = { id = usa_news.29 }#check if needs new loc
		USA = { add_timed_idea = { idea = USA_alaska_purchase_usa days = 365 } }
		USA = { transfer_state = 463 }
		USA = {
			unlock_national_focus = USA_diplomacy_alaska #######################
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_mormon_unrest
				value = -5
		}
	}
	option = {

			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = SPR }
			}

			set_global_flag = cuba_sold_not_by_spain
		}
		set_global_flag = USACuba_Purchased

			limit = { TAG = SPR }
			add_stability = -0.10
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -9
				TAG = SPR
			}

				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = usa.219
	title = usa.219.t
	desc = {
		text = usa.219.d1
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_covode_committee
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = usa.219.d2
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_close_ranks
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_german_reichstag_gathering

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa.219"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = usa.219.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa.219.a"
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_covode_committee
		}
		set_country_flag = breckinridge_sucessor
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_covode_committee
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_democracy
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_democracy
				popularity = -0.025
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.219.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa.219.b"
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = USA_close_ranks
		}
		set_country_flag = douglas_successor
		add_political_power = 100
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_covode_committee
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = traditional_conservatism
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = traditional_conservatism
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = usa.219.c
		# log = "option:		name = usa.219.c"
		set_country_flag = buchanan_successor
		add_political_power = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = USA_covode_committee
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_democracy
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_democracy
				popularity = -0.025
			}
		}
	}
}

# Independence Day #
country_event = {
	id = usa_flavor.23
	title = usa_flavor.23.t
	desc = usa_flavor.23.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_independence_day

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_flavor.23"
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_flavor.23"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = usa_flavor.23
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = usa_flavor.23.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_flavor.23.a"
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet = no
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		add_political_power = 25
	}
	option = {
		name = usa_flavor.23.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa_flavor.23.b"
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					is_puppet = yes
					is_subject = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.01
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = centrism
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = traditional_conservatism
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_egalitarianism
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
}

	title = usa_flavor.30.t
	desc = usa_flavor.30.d
	picture = GFX_comstock_event_pic

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = usa_flavor.30.a
		add_resource = {
			type = valuables
			amount = 1
			state = 379
		}
		379 = {
			add_manpower = 1000
		}
	}
}

#Alaska Purchase
news_event = {
		id = usa_news.17
		title = usa_news.17.t
		desc = {
			text = usa_news.17.d
			trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus } }
		}
		desc = {
			text = usa_news.17.d_notrus
			trigger = { has_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus }
		}

		picture = GFX_news_event_usa_alaska

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing  = usa_news.17"
	}

		major = yes

		is_triggered_only = yes

		option = {
			trigger = {
				tag = USA
			}
			name = usa_news.17.a
		# log = "option:			name = usa_news.17.a"
			clr_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus
			clear_global_event_target = alaska_sold_not_by_rus
		}
		option = {
			trigger = {
				tag = RUS
			}
			name = usa_news.17.b
		# log = "option:			name = usa_news.17.b"
		}
		option = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = { tag = USA }
				NOT = { tag = RUS }
			}
			name = usa_news.17.c
		# log = "option:			name = usa_news.17.c"
		}
}

	desc = {

		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus } }
	}
	desc = {

		trigger = { has_global_flag = alaska_sold_not_by_rus }
	}

	picture = GFX_news_event_usa_alaska

	immediate = {

		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}

	option = {

			tag = RUS

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We can agree to these terms
		name = usa_diplomacy.2.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_diplomacy.2.a"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = USA
					ratio > 1
				}
				add = 21
			}
			modifier = {
				naval_strength_ratio = {
					tag = USA
					ratio > 1
				}
				add = 21
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { debt_level > 30 }
				add = 23
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Absolutely not
		name = usa_diplomacy.2.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa_diplomacy.2.b"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 99
		}
	}
}

country_event = {#player decides whether to pursue the hot pig war
	id = usa_diplomacy.11
	title = usa_diplomacy.11.t
	desc = usa_diplomacy.11.d
	picture = GFX_event_clayton_conspiracy_start

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #commit to going hot pig-war later
		name = usa_diplomacy.11.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_diplomacy.11.a"
		set_country_flag = clayton_conspiracy_participant
		set_country_flag = clayton_stage_1
		activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_mission
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = britain.186
				days = 60
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				decision_days_var = 28
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1858.2.1
				}
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 190
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1858.4.15
				}
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 180
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1858.7.1
				}
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 170
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1858.9.15
				}
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 160
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					date < 1858.12.1
				}
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 150
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = {
					days_var = 140
				}
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = {
			target = USA
			decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_delay_1
		}
		complete_national_focus = USA_focus_clayton_conspiracy
	}
	option = { #accept british colonial claims
		name = usa_diplomacy.11.b
		# log = "option:		name = usa_diplomacy.11.b"
	}
}

				has_country_flag = clayton_stage_2
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa_diplomacy.12.d3
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = clayton_stage_3
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = usa_diplomacy.12.d4
		trigger = {
			USA = {
				has_country_flag = clayton_stage_4
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		create_faction = USA_clayton_conspiracy_faction
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = global_flag_hot_pig_war
		}
		country_event = USA_clayton_conspiracy.50
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #war to distract from internal issues
		name = usa_diplomacy.12.a
		# log = "option:		name = usa_diplomacy.12.a"
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ENG
			type = take_claimed_state
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = clayton_stage_4
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = BCO
				type = take_state
			}
		}
		activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_seize_claims_war_mission_USA
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = utahWarOngoing
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = USA_mormon_unrest
						value = 7
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = 5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = USA_mormon_unrest
					value = -5
				}
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			country_event = usa_diplomacy.13
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.51
				days = 3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {#removing missions/decisions
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_delay_1
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_invite_NIC
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_invite_HON
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_delay_2
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_invite_GUA
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_delay_3
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_invite_VEN
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_equipment
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_request_military_access
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_boat
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_cash
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA
				decision = USA_mission_clayton_conspiracy_extradite_walker
			}
			remove_targeted_decision = {
				target = USA

	id = usa_diplomacy.15
	title = usa_diplomacy.15.t
	desc = usa_diplomacy.15.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Send a large amount of arms and some generals
		name = usa_diplomacy.15.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment > 4999
				}
				OR = {
					USA_character_george_h_thomas = {
						OR = {
							is_corps_commander = yes
							is_field_marshal = yes
						}
					}
					USA_character_philip_sheridan = {
						OR = {
							is_corps_commander = yes
							is_field_marshal = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = usa_gilded_sent_generals_to_mexican_libs_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA_character_george_h_thomas = {
					OR = {
						is_corps_commander = yes
						is_field_marshal = yes
					}
				}
			}
			USA_character_george_h_thomas = {
				set_nationality = MEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				USA_character_philip_sheridan = {
					OR = {
						is_corps_commander = yes
						is_field_marshal = yes
					}
				}
			}
			USA_character_philip_sheridan = {
				set_nationality = MEX
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -5000
			producer = USA
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			MEX = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 5000
					producer = USA
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = usa_large_military_support_to_mex

			country_event = usa_diplomacy.16
		}
	}
	option = { # Send a large amount of arms

			}

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = usa_promised_chihuahua_back_to_mex
		MEX = {
			country_event = usa_diplomacy.33
		}
	}
	option = { # We can give them back both
		name = usa_diplomacy.31.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					482 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
					483 = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = usa_promised_sonora_back_to_mex
		set_country_flag = usa_promised_chihuahua_back_to_mex
		MEX = {
			country_event = usa_diplomacy.34
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #NIC replies yes
	id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.5
	title = USA_clayton_conspiracy.5.t
	desc = USA_clayton_conspiracy.5.d
	# picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.5.a
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NIC
			modifier = usa_opinion_clayton_conspiracy_participant
		}
		NIC = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = USA
				modifier = usa_opinion_clayton_conspiracy_participant
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = clayton_stage_2 }
			activate_targeted_decision = {
				target = FROM
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_equipment
			}

				target = FROM
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_cash
			}

				target = FROM
				decision = USA_decision_clayton_request_military_access
			}
			FROM = {
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = USA
					decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_request_equipment
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = USA

				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = ENG
					decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_recon_british
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = FROM
					decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_propaganda_campaign
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = clayton_stage_3 }

				}

				}
				activate_targeted_decision = {
					target = FROM
					decision = USA_decision_clayton_conspiracy_secret_conscription
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {

			}
