country_event = { #Distribute equipment
	id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20
	title = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20.t
	desc = {
		text = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20.d1
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_requesting_clayton_equipment@FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20.d2
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
	}
	# picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20"
		set_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@infantry_equipment
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@uniform_equipment
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = cav_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@cavalry_equipment
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = can_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@field_artillery_equipment
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = howie_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@howitzer_artillery_equipment
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = sup_equip_total
			value = num_equipment@support_equipment
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = cav_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = can_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = howie_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = sup_equip_total
			value = 0.01
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total_med
			value = inf_equip_total
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total_lg
			value = inf_equip_total
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total_med
			value = uni_equip_total
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total_lg
			value = uni_equip_total
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total_med
			value = 2
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total_med
			value = 2
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = inf_equip_total_lg
			value = 3
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = uni_equip_total_lg
			value = 3
		}
	}

	option = { #small
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20.a
		send_equipment = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = inf_equip_total
			target = FROM
		}
		send_equipment = {
			type = uniform_equipment
			amount = uni_equip_total
			target = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = USA
				modifier = usa_opinion_clayton_conspiracy_sent_weapon_aid_1
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = USA_clayton_willingness_var
			value = 1
		}
		USA_scripted_effect_clayton_change_willingness = yes
		# hidden_effect = {
		# 	activate_targeted_decision = {
		# 		target = FROM
		# 		decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_equipment
		# 	}
		# }
		# FROM = {
		# 	country_event = {
		# 		id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.26
		# 		days = 1
		# 	}
		# }
	}

	option = { #medium
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.20.b
		send_equipment = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = inf_equip_total_med
			target = FROM
		}
		send_equipment = {
			type = uniform_equipment
			amount = uni_equip_total_med
			target = FROM
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				send_equipment = {
					type = cavalry_equipment
					amount = cav_equip_total
					target = FROM
				}
			}
			10 = {
				send_equipment = {
					type = field_artillery_equipment
					amount = can_equip_total
					target = FROM
				}				
			}
			0 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							howie_equip_total > 0
						}
						stockpile_ratio = {
							archetype = howitzer_artillery_equipment
							ratio > 0
						}
					}
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = howitzer_artillery_equipment
					amount = howie_equip_total
					target = FROM
				}				
			}
			0 = {
				modifier = {
					add = 10
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							sup_equip_total > 0
						}
						stockpile_ratio = {
							archetype = support_equipment
							ratio > 0
						}
					}
				}
				send_equipment = {
					type = support_equipment
					amount = sup_equip_total
					target = FROM
				}				
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = USA
				modifier = usa_opinion_clayton_conspiracy_sent_weapon_aid_2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = USA_clayton_willingness_var
			value = 2
		}
		USA_scripted_effect_clayton_change_willingness = yes
		# hidden_effect = {
		# 	activate_targeted_decision = {
		# 		target = FROM
		# 		decision = USA_decision_clayton_send_equipment
		# 	}
		# }
		# FROM = {
		# 	country_event = {
		# 		id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.26
		# 		days = 1
		# 	}
		# }
		clear_variable = inf_equip_total
		clear_variable = uni_equip_total
		clear_variable = inf_equip_total_med
		clear_variable = uni_equip_total_med
		clear_variable = inf_equip_total_lg
		clear_variable = uni_equip_total_lg
		clear_variable = cav_equip_total
		clear_variable = can_equip_total
		clear_variable = howie_equip_total
		clear_variable = sup_equip_total
	}

	option = { #large

			target = FROM

		multiply_variable = {

			value = 2
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = can_equip_total
			value = 2

		multiply_variable = {
			var = howie_equip_total
			value = 2
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			var = sup_equip_total
			value = 2
		}
		random_list = {
			10 = {
				send_equipment = {
					type = cavalry_equipment
					amount = cav_equip_total
					target = FROM

			}

country_event = {#transferring boat(s) to conspirators
	id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23
	title = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23.t
	desc = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23.d
	#picture = 

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23"
	}

	option = {
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23.a
		transfer_ship = {
			type = corvette
			target = FROM
			exclude_refitting = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = clayton_conspiracy_send_boat_tt
		random_list = {
			5 = {
				transfer_ship = {
					type = corvette
					target = FROM
					exclude_refitting = yes
				}
				transfer_ship = {
					type = corvette
					target = FROM
					exclude_refitting = yes
				}
			}
			5 = {
				modifier = {
					add = -5
					check_variable = { num_ships_with_type@gunboat > 0 }
				}
				transfer_ship = {
					type = gunboat
					target = FROM
					exclude_refitting = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.23.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { num_ships_with_type@frigate > 0 }
			has_country_flag = clayton_stage_4
		}
		transfer_ship = {
			type = frigate
			target = FROM
			exclude_refitting = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #US hears ally request mil support
	id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30
	title = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30.t
	desc = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30.d
	#picture = 

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30"
	}

	option = {
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = NIC }
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_military_support_mission_NIC
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = HON }
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_military_support_mission_HON
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = GUA }
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_military_support_mission_GUA
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { tag = VEN }
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_military_support_mission_VEN
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA_clayton_conspiracy.30.b
	}
}

			}
		}

			limit = {

			}

country_event = { #hidden event to add all participants to war
	id = USA_clayton_conspiracy.51

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NIC = {
					has_country_flag = clayton_conspiracy_participant
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				USA = {
					add_to_faction = NIC
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = USA
				enemy = ENG
				hostility_reason = asked_to_join
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_seize_claims_war_mission_allies
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				HON = {
					has_country_flag = clayton_conspiracy_participant
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				USA = {
					add_to_faction = HON
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = USA
				enemy = ENG
				hostility_reason = asked_to_join
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_seize_claims_war_mission_allies
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GUA = {
					has_country_flag = clayton_conspiracy_participant
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				USA = {
					add_to_faction = GUA
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = USA
				enemy = ENG
				hostility_reason = asked_to_join
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_seize_claims_war_mission_allies
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VEN = {
					has_country_flag = clayton_conspiracy_participant
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				USA = {
					add_to_faction = VEN
				}
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = USA
				enemy = ENG
				hostility_reason = asked_to_join
			}
			activate_mission = USA_clayton_conspiracy_seize_claims_war_mission_allies
		}
	}

}

### GILDED AGE ###

country_event = { # Event about the Robber Barons
	id = usa_gilded_age.1
	title = usa_gilded_age.1.t
	desc = usa_gilded_age.1.desc
	picture = placeholder
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Captains of Industry
		name = usa_gilded_age.1.a
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			value = 4
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			value = 4
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_opinion
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_opinion_oil_4
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_opinion_steel_4
	}
	option = { # ...or Robber Barons?
		name = usa_gilded_age.1.b
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_influence
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_steel_influence
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_influence
			value = 2
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_standard_oil_influence
			min = 0
			max = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_influence_steel_2
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_influence_oil_2
	}
}

		}

	}

	immediate = {

	}
		is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		# log = "[THIS.GetTag]: firing = usa_debug.9"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate = token:USA_character_ulysses_s_grant }
			set_variable = { usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate_sub_ideology = token:liberal_social }
		}
	}
	option = {
				name = usa_debug.9.b
		# log = "option:				name = usa_debug.9.b"
		meta_effect = {
			debug = yes
			text = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = ""
						expire = "2050.1.1.2"
						ideology = [usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate_sub_ideology]
					}
				}
			}
			usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate = "[?usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate.GetTokenKey]"
			usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate_sub_ideology = "[?usa_social_egalitarianism_candidate_sub_ideology.GetTokenKey]"
		}
